      1 +using Godot;
      2 +using slime.data;
      3 +using System;
      4 +using System.Collections.Generic;
      5 +using System.Text.Json;
      6 +
      7 +/// <summary>
      8 +/// Runtime Data typed contract 验证场景。
      9 +/// </summary>
     10 +public partial class RuntimeDataValidationScene : Node
     11 +{
     12 +    private int _total;
     13 +    private int _failed;
     14 +
     15 +    public override void _Ready()
     16 +    {
     17 +        RunAll();
     18 +        if (_failed == 0)
     19 +        {
     20 +            GD.Print($"[PASS] RuntimeDataValidationScene total={_total}");
     21 +            GetTree().Quit(0);
     22 +            return;
     23 +        }
     24 +
     25 +        GD.PrintErr($"[FAIL] RuntimeDataValidationScene failed={_failed} total={_total}");
     26 +        GetTree().Quit(1);
     27 +    }
     28 +
     29 +    private void RunAll()
     30 +    {
     31 +        TestTypedSetGetTryHasRemove();
     32 +        TestModifierConstraints();
     33 +        TestComputedDirtyCache();
     34 +        TestCategoryReset();
     35 +        TestDataChangePayload();
     36 +        TestTypedSnapshotApply();
     37 +        TestSnapshotInvalidCases();
     38 +    }
     39 +
     40 +    private void TestTypedSetGetTryHasRemove()
     41 +    {
     42 +        var data = new Data();
     43 +        data.Set(DataKey.BaseHp, 100f);
     44 +
     45 +        AssertEqual("typed.get", data.Get(DataKey.BaseHp), 100f);
     46 +        AssertTrue("typed.tryget", data.TryGet(DataKey.BaseHp, out var hp) && Math.Abs(hp - 100f) < 0.001f);
     47 +        AssertTrue("typed.has", data.Has(DataKey.BaseHp));
     48 +        AssertTrue("typed.remove", data.Remove(DataKey.BaseHp));
     49 +        AssertFalse("typed.has.after.remove", data.Has(DataKey.BaseHp));
     50 +    }
     51 +
     52 +    private void TestModifierConstraints()
     53 +    {
     54 +        var data = new Data();
     55 +        data.Set(DataKey.BaseHp, 100f);
     56 +        AssertTrue("modifier.numeric.allowed", data.AddModifier(DataKey.BaseHp, new DataModifier(ModifierType.Additive, 25f, id: "hp-bonus")));
     57 +        AssertEqual("modifier.numeric.value", data.Get(DataKey.BaseHp), 125f);
     58 +
     59 +        data.Set(DataKey.Name, "hero");
     60 +        AssertFalse("modifier.string.rejected", data.AddModifier(DataKey.Name, new DataModifier(ModifierType.Additive, 1f, id: "bad")));
     61 +        AssertEqual("modifier.string.unchanged", data.Get(DataKey.Name), "hero");
     62 +    }
     63 +
     64 +    private void TestComputedDirtyCache()
     65 +    {
     66 +        var data = new Data();
     67 +        data.Set(DataKey.BaseHp, 100f);
     68 +        data.Set(DataKey.HpBonus, 25f);
     69 +        AssertEqual("computed.initial", data.Get(DataKey.FinalHp), 125f);
     70 +
     71 +        data.Set(DataKey.HpBonus, 50f);
     72 +        AssertEqual("computed.dirty.after.dependency", data.Get(DataKey.FinalHp), 150f);
     73 +    }
     74 +
     75 +    private void TestCategoryReset()
     76 +    {
     77 +        var data = new Data();
     78 +        data.Set(DataKey.BaseHp, 777f);
     79 +        data.Set(DataKey.Name, "keep");
     80 +
     81 +        data.ResetByCategory(DataCategory_Attribute.Health);
     82 +        AssertEqual("category.reset.health", data.Get(DataKey.BaseHp), DataKey.BaseHp.DefaultValue);
     83 +        AssertEqual("category.reset.other.category.kept", data.Get(DataKey.Name), "keep");
     84 +    }
     85 +
     86 +    private void TestDataChangePayload()
     87 +    {
     88 +        var entity = new ValidationEntity();
     89 +        GameEventType.Data.PropertyChangedEventData? seen = null;
     90 +        entity.Events.On<GameEventType.Data.PropertyChangedEventData>(
     91 +            GameEventType.Data.PropertyChanged,
     92 +            evt => seen = evt);
     93 +
     94 +        entity.Data.Set(DataKey.BaseHp, 10f);
     95 +
     96 +        AssertTrue("change.payload.seen", seen.HasValue);
     97 +        AssertEqual("change.payload.key", seen!.Value.Key, DataKey.BaseHp.Key);
     98 +        AssertEqual("change.payload.new", (float)seen.Value.NewValue!, 10f);
     99 +    }
    100 +
    101 +    private void TestTypedSnapshotApply()
    102 +    {
    103 +        var document = RuntimeDataSnapshot.ParseTypedSnapshot(BuildValidSnapshot());
    104 +        var data = new Data();
    105 +        var report = RuntimeDataSnapshot.ApplyRecordToData(document, "unit.player", "player.validation", data);
    106 +
    107 +        AssertTrue("snapshot.apply.success", report.Success);
    108 +        AssertEqual("snapshot.apply.name", data.Get(DataKey.Name), "验证玩家");
    109 +        AssertEqual("snapshot.apply.hp", data.Get(DataKey.BaseHp), 120f);
    110 +    }
    111 +
    112 +    private void TestSnapshotInvalidCases()
    113 +    {
    114 +        AssertSnapshotError("snapshot.unknown_key", BuildSnapshotWithField("Unknown.Key", "float", 1f));
    115 +        AssertSnapshotError("snapshot.missing_descriptor", BuildSnapshotWithMissingDescriptor());
    116 +        AssertSnapshotError("snapshot.wrong_type", BuildSnapshotWithField(DataKey.BaseHp.Key, "float", "bad"));
    117 +        AssertSnapshotError("snapshot.default_drift", BuildSnapshotWithDefaultDrift());
    118 +        AssertSnapshotError("snapshot.resource_disabled_capability", BuildSnapshotWithDisabledResource());
    119 +    }
    120 +
    121 +    private void AssertSnapshotError(string expectedCode, string json)
    122 +    {
    123 +        var document = RuntimeDataSnapshot.ParseTypedSnapshot(json);
    124 +        var report = RuntimeDataSnapshot.ApplyRecordToData(document, "unit.player", "player.validation", new Data());
    125 +        AssertFalse(expectedCode, report.Success);
    126 +        AssertTrue(expectedCode + ".reported", report.Errors.Exists(error => error.Code == expectedCode));
    127 +    }
    128 +
    129 +    private static string BuildValidSnapshot()
    130 +    {
    131 +        return """
    132 +        {
    133 +          "schemaVersion": 1,
    134 +          "generatedAtUtc": "2026-05-22T00:00:00Z",
    135 +          "manifest": { "profile": "slimeainew", "catalogId": "slimeainew", "enabledCapabilities": ["unit"] },
    136 +          "descriptors": [
    137 +            { "key": "Name", "type": "string", "defaultValue": "" },
    138 +            { "key": "BaseHp", "type": "float", "defaultValue": 10 }
    139 +          ],
    140 +          "records": [
    141 +            {
    142 +              "table": "unit.player",
    143 +              "id": "player.validation",
    144 +              "name": "验证玩家",
    145 +              "fields": {
    146 +                "Name": { "type": "string", "value": "验证玩家" },
    147 +                "BaseHp": { "type": "float", "value": 120 }
    148 +              }
    149 +            }
    150 +          ],
    151 +          "resources": []
    152 +        }
    153 +        """;
    154 +    }
    155 +
    156 +    private static string BuildSnapshotWithField(string key, string type, object? value)
    157 +    {
    158 +        using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(BuildValidSnapshot());
    159 +        var valueLiteral = value is string text ? $"\"{text}\"" : Convert.ToString(value, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
    160 +        return $$"""
    161 +        {
    162 +          "schemaVersion": 1,
    163 +          "generatedAtUtc": "2026-05-22T00:00:00Z",
    164 +          "manifest": { "profile": "slimeainew", "catalogId": "slimeainew", "enabledCapabilities": ["unit"] },
    165 +          "descriptors": [
    166 +            { "key": "{{key}}", "type": "{{type}}", "defaultValue": 0 }
    167 +          ],
    168 +          "records": [
    169 +            { "table": "unit.player", "id": "player.validation", "name": "验证玩家", "fields": { "{{key}}": { "type": "{{type}}", "value": {{valueLitera
         l}} } } }
    170 +          ],
    171 +          "resources": []
    172 +        }
    173 +        """;
    174 +    }
    175 +
    176 +    private static string BuildSnapshotWithMissingDescriptor()
    177 +    {
    178 +        return """
    179 +        {
    180 +          "schemaVersion": 1,
    181 +          "generatedAtUtc": "2026-05-22T00:00:00Z",
    182 +          "manifest": { "profile": "slimeainew", "catalogId": "slimeainew", "enabledCapabilities": ["unit"] },
    183 +          "descriptors": [],
    184 +          "records": [
    185 +            { "table": "unit.player", "id": "player.validation", "name": "验证玩家", "fields": { "BaseHp": { "type": "float", "value": 120 } } }
    186 +          ],
    187 +          "resources": []
    188 +        }
    189 +        """;
    190 +    }
    191 +
    192 +    private static string BuildSnapshotWithDefaultDrift()
    193 +    {
    194 +        return """
    195 +        {
    196 +          "schemaVersion": 1,

    230 +    private void AssertEqual<T>(string name, T actual, T expected)
    231 +    {
    232 +        _total++;
    233 +        if (EqualityComparer<T>.Default.Equals(actual, expected))
    234 +        {
    235 +            GD.Print($"[PASS] {name}");
    236 +            return;
    237 +        }
    238 +
    239 +        _failed++;
    240 +        GD.PrintErr($"[FAIL] {name}: expected={expected} actual={actual}");
    241 +    }
    242 +
    243 +    private void AssertTrue(string name, bool condition)
    244 +    {
    245 +        AssertEqual(name, condition, true);
    246 +    }
    247 +
    248 +    private void AssertFalse(string name, bool condition)
    249 +    {
    250 +        AssertEqual(name, condition, false);
    251 +    }
    252 +

    257 +
    258 +        public ValidationEntity()
    259 +        {
    260 +            Data = new Data(this);
    261 +        }
    262 +    }

     1 +using System;
     2 +using System.Collections.Generic;
     3 +using System.Linq;
     4 +
     5 +/// <summary>
     6 +/// Runtime Data catalog，负责 stable key 到 typed key/id 的冻结解析。
     7 +/// </summary>
     8 +public sealed class DataCatalog
     9 +{
    10 +    private readonly Dictionary<string, IDataKey> _byStableKey;
    11 +    private readonly Dictionary<string, int> _ids;
    12 +
    13 +    internal DataCatalog(IEnumerable<IDataKey> keys)
    14 +    {
    15 +        _byStableKey = new Dictionary<string, IDataKey>(StringComparer.Ordinal);
    16 +        _ids = new Dictionary<string, int>(StringComparer.Ordinal);
    17 +
    18 +        int id = 0;
    19 +        foreach (var key in keys.OrderBy(k => k.Key, StringComparer.Ordinal))
    20 +        {
    21 +            if (_byStableKey.ContainsKey(key.Key))
    22 +            {
    23 +                continue;
    24 +            }
    25 +
    26 +            _byStableKey.Add(key.Key, key);
    27 +            _ids.Add(key.Key, id++);
    28 +        }
    29 +    }
    30 +
    31 +    public IReadOnlyCollection<IDataKey> Keys => _byStableKey.Values;
    32 +
    33 +    public bool TryResolve(string stableKey, out IDataKey key)
    34 +    {
    35 +        return _byStableKey.TryGetValue(stableKey, out key!);
    36 +    }
    37 +
    38 +    public bool TryResolve<T>(string stableKey, out DataKey<T> key)
    39 +    {
    40 +        if (_byStableKey.TryGetValue(stableKey, out var raw) && raw is DataKey<T> typed)
    41 +        {
    42 +            key = typed;
    43 +            return true;
    44 +        }
    45 +
    46 +        key = null!;
    47 +        return false;
    48 +    }
    49 +
    50 +    public int GetId(IDataKey key)
    51 +    {
    52 +        return _ids.TryGetValue(key.Key, out var id) ? id : -1;
    53 +    }
    54 +}
    55 +
    56 +/// <summary>
    57 +/// Runtime Data catalog builder。
    58 +/// </summary>
    59 +public sealed class DataCatalogBuilder
    60 +{
    61 +    private readonly List<IDataKey> _keys = [];
    62 +
    63 +    public DataCatalogBuilder Add(IDataKey key)
    64 +    {
    65 +        _keys.Add(key);
    66 +        return this;
    67 +    }
    68 +
    69 +    public DataCatalog Build()
    70 +    {
    71 +        return new DataCatalog(_keys);
    72 +    }
    73 +}

• Edited SlimeAINew/Src/ECS/Base/Data/Data.cs (+85 -0)
    699
    700 +    private bool TrySetSlotUntyped(IDataKey key, object? value)
    701 +    {
    702 +        if (key is not DataMeta meta)
    703 +        {
    704 +            return false;
    705 +        }
    706 +
    707 +        if (meta.HasOptions && value != null && !meta.IsValidOption(value))
    708 +        {
    709 +            _log.Error($"无效的选项值: {key.Key} = {value}");
    710 +            return false;
    711 +        }
    712 +
    713 +        var converted = ConvertValueBoxed(value ?? key.UntypedDefaultValue!, key.ValueType, key.UntypedDefaultValue!);
    714 +        converted = meta.Clamp(converted);
    715 +        var keyId = _catalog.GetId(key);
    716 +        if (keyId < 0)
    717 +        {
    718 +            _log.Error($"DataKey 未注册到 catalog: {key.Key}");
    719 +            return false;
    720 +        }
    721 +
    722 +        object? oldValue = null;
    723 +        if (_slots.TryGetValue(keyId, out var slot))
    724 +        {
    725 +            oldValue = slot.UntypedValue;
    726 +            if (Equals(oldValue, converted))
    727 +            {
    728 +                return false;
    729 +            }
    730 +
    731 +            slot.UntypedValue = converted;
    732 +        }
    733 +        else
    734 +        {
    735 +            var slotType = typeof(DataSlot<>).MakeGenericType(key.ValueType);
    736 +            slot = (IDataSlot)Activator.CreateInstance(slotType, key, converted)!;
    737 +            _slots[keyId] = slot;
    738 +        }
    739 +
    740 +        MarkDirty(key.Key);
    741 +        NotifyChanged(key.Key, oldValue, converted);
    742 +        return true;
    743 +    }
    744 +
    745 +    private bool RemoveUntyped(IDataKey key)
    746 +    {
    747 +        var keyId = _catalog.GetId(key);
    748 +        if (keyId >= 0 && _slots.TryGetValue(keyId, out var oldSlot))
    749 +        {
    750 +            _slots.Remove(keyId);
    751 +            _modifiers.Remove(key.Key);
    752 +            _cachedValues.Remove(key.Key);
    753 +            _dirtyKeys.Remove(key.Key);
    754 +            NotifyChanged(key.Key, oldSlot.UntypedValue, null);
    755 +            return true;
    756 +        }
    757 +
    758 +        return false;
    759 +    }
    760 +
    761 +    private object? GetUntyped(IDataKey key)
    762 +    {
    763 +        if (key.IsComputed && key is DataMeta meta)
    764 +        {
    765 +            return GetComputedValueBoxed(key.Key, meta, key.UntypedDefaultValue!, key.ValueType);
    766 +        }
    767 +
    768 +        var baseValue = GetUntypedBase(key);
    769 +        if (key.SupportsModifiers && baseValue != null && _modifiers.ContainsKey(key.Key))
    770 +        {
    771 +            return GetModifiedValueBoxed(key.Key, baseValue, key.UntypedDefaultValue!, key.ValueType);
    772 +        }
    773 +
    774 +        return baseValue ?? key.UntypedDefaultValue;
    775 +    }
    776 +
    777 +    private object? GetUntypedBase(IDataKey key)
    778 +    {
    779 +        var keyId = _catalog.GetId(key);
    780 +        return keyId >= 0 && _slots.TryGetValue(keyId, out var slot)
    781 +            ? slot.UntypedValue
    782 +            : key.UntypedDefaultValue;
    783 +    }

     96 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'TargetingIndicatorData', 'unit.targeting_indicator', id, name, 'IsInvulnerable', 'bool', CASE is_invulnerable WHEN 1 THEN 'true' E
         LSE 'false' END, 'unit_targeting_indicator', id, 'is_invulnerable' FROM unit_targeting_indicator
     97 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'TargetingIndicatorData', 'unit.targeting_indicator', id, name, 'MoveSpeed', 'float', CAST(move_speed AS TEXT), 'unit_targeting_ind
         icator', id, 'move_speed' FROM unit_targeting_indicator
     98 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'TargetingIndicatorData', 'unit.targeting_indicator', id, name, 'BaseAttackSpeed', 'float', '0', 'unit_targeting_indicator', id, 'b
         ase_attack_speed' FROM unit_targeting_indicator
     99 +
    100 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'Name', 'string', name, 'ability
         ', id, 'name' FROM ability
    101 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityFeatureGroup', 'string',
          feature_group_id, 'ability', id, 'feature_group_id' FROM ability
    102 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'FeatureHandlerId', 'string', fe

    103 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'Description', 'string', descrip
         tion, 'ability', id, 'description' FROM ability
    104 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityIcon', 'string', icon_pa
         th, 'ability', id, 'icon_path' FROM ability
    105 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'EntityType', 'string', entity_t

    106 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityType', 'string', ability

    109 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityCostAmount', 'float', CA

    110 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityCooldown', 'float', CAST

    112 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'IsAbilityUsesCharges', 'bool',

    113 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityMaxCharges', 'int', CAST

    114 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityChargeTime', 'float', CA

    115 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityTargetSelection', 'strin
         g', target_selection, 'ability', id, 'target_selection' FROM ability
    116 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityCastRange', 'float', CAS
         T(cast_range AS TEXT), 'ability', id, 'cast_range' FROM ability
    117 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityEffectRadius', 'float',

    119 +    UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN chain_count IS NULL THEN 'AbilityData' ELSE 'ChainAbilityData' END, 'ability', id, name, 'ProjectileScene', 'string', COA
         LESCE(projectile_scene_path, ''), 'ability', id, 'projectile_scene_path' FROM ability
    120 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'ChainAbilityData', 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityChainCount', 'int', CAST(chain_count AS TEXT), 'ability', id, 'chain_count' FROM a
         bility WHERE chain_count IS NOT NULL
    121 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'ChainAbilityData', 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityChainRange', 'float', CAST(chain_range AS TEXT), 'ability', id, 'chain_range' FROM
          ability WHERE chain_range IS NOT NULL
    122 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'ChainAbilityData', 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityChainDelay', 'float', CAST(chain_delay AS TEXT), 'ability', id, 'chain_delay' FROM
          ability WHERE chain_delay IS NOT NULL
    123 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'ChainAbilityData', 'ability', id, name, 'AbilityChainDamageDecay', 'float', CAST(chain_damage_decay AS TEXT), 'ability', id, 'chai
         n_damage_decay' FROM ability WHERE chain_damage_decay IS NOT NULL
    124 +
    125 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'SystemId', 'string', system_id, 'system_config', id, 'system_id' FROM system_config
    126 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'MountGroup', 'string', mount_group, 'system_config', id, 'mount_group' FROM system_c
         onfig
    127 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'Tags', 'string', tags, 'system_config', id, 'tags' FROM system_config
    128 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'Required', 'bool', CASE required WHEN 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END, 'system_config
         ', id, 'required' FROM system_config
    129 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'AutoLoad', 'bool', CASE auto_load WHEN 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END, 'system_confi
         g', id, 'auto_load' FROM system_config
    130 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'StartEnabled', 'bool', CASE start_enabled WHEN 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END, 'syst
         em_config', id, 'start_enabled' FROM system_config
    131 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'Priority', 'int', CAST(priority AS TEXT), 'system_config', id, 'priority' FROM syste
         m_config
    132 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'AllowedFlowStates', 'string', allowed_flow_states, 'system_config', id, 'allowed_flo
         w_states' FROM system_config
    133 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'RequiredOverlays', 'string', required_overlays, 'system_config', id, 'required_overl
         ays' FROM system_config
    134 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'BlockedOverlays', 'string', blocked_overlays, 'system_config', id, 'blocked_overlays
         ' FROM system_config
    135 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'AllowedSimulationStates', 'string', allowed_simulation_states, 'system_config', id,
         'allowed_simulation_states' FROM system_config
    136 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'Dependencies', 'string_array', dependencies, 'system_config', id, 'dependencies' FRO
         M system_config
    137 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemData', 'system.config', id, system_id, 'Description', 'string', description, 'system_config', id, 'description' FROM system_
         config
    138 +
    139 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'PresetName', 'string', preset_name, 'system_preset', id, 'preset_name' FROM
         system_preset
    140 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'IsActive', 'bool', CASE is_active WHEN 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END, 'syst
         em_preset', id, 'is_active' FROM system_preset
    141 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'EnabledTags', 'string', enabled_tags, 'system_preset', id, 'enabled_tags' FR
         OM system_preset
    142 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'EnabledSystemIds', 'string_array', enabled_system_ids, 'system_preset', id,
         'enabled_system_ids' FROM system_preset
    143 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'DisabledSystemIds', 'string_array', disabled_system_ids, 'system_preset', id
         , 'disabled_system_ids' FROM system_preset
    144 +    UNION ALL SELECT 'SystemPresetData', 'system.preset', id, preset_name, 'Description', 'string', description, 'system_preset', id, 'description' FROM
          system_preset
    145 +),
    146 +descriptor_source AS (
    147 +    SELECT
    148 +        field_key,
    149 +        CASE
    150 +            WHEN field_key IN ('Name', 'Description', 'Id', 'SourceEntityId', 'OriginEntityId') THEN 'Base'
    151 +            WHEN field_key IN ('Team', 'EntityType', 'DeathType', 'VisualScenePath', 'Level', 'UnitRank', 'IsShowHealthBar', 'IsEnableSpawnRule',
    152 +                'SpawnStrategy', 'SpawnMinWave', 'SpawnMaxWave', 'SpawnInterval', 'SpawnMaxCountPerWave', 'SingleSpawnCount',
    153 +                'SingleSpawnVariance', 'SpawnStartDelay', 'SpawnWeight', 'HealthBarHeight', 'ExpReward', 'IsDead', 'IsInvulnerable') THEN 'Unit'
    154 +            WHEN field_key IN ('DetectionRange') THEN 'AI'
    155 +            WHEN field_key IN ('BaseHp', 'BaseHpRegen', 'LifeSteal', 'BaseAttack', 'BaseAttackSpeed', 'AttackRange', 'CritRate',
    156 +                'CritDamage', 'Penetration', 'BaseDefense', 'DamageReduction', 'MoveSpeed', 'DodgeChance', 'PickupRange') THEN 'Attribute'
    157 +            WHEN field_key IN ('AbilityFeatureGroup', 'AbilityIcon', 'AbilityType', 'AbilityLevel', 'AbilityMaxLevel', 'AbilityDamage',
    158 +                'AbilityDamageBonus', 'CooldownReduction', 'AbilityCooldown', 'IsAbilityUsesCharges', 'AbilityMaxCharges',
    159 +                'AbilityChargeTime', 'AbilityCostType', 'AbilityCostAmount', 'AbilityTriggerMode', 'AbilityTargetSelection',
    160 +                'AbilityCastRange', 'AbilityEffectRadius', 'AbilityChainCount', 'AbilityChainRange', 'AbilityChainDelay',
    161 +                'AbilityChainDamageDecay', 'EffectScene', 'ProjectileScene') THEN 'Ability'
    162 +            WHEN field_key IN ('FeatureHandlerId') THEN 'Feature'
    163 +            WHEN field_key IN ('SystemId', 'MountGroup', 'Tags', 'Required', 'AutoLoad', 'StartEnabled', 'Priority',
    164 +                'AllowedFlowStates', 'RequiredOverlays', 'BlockedOverlays', 'AllowedSimulationStates', 'Dependencies',
    165 +                'PresetName', 'IsActive', 'EnabledTags', 'EnabledSystemIds', 'DisabledSystemIds') THEN 'System'
    166 +            ELSE 'shared'
    167 +        END AS owner_capability,
    168 +        value_type AS descriptor_type,
    169 +        CASE field_key
    170 +            WHEN 'Name' THEN ''
    171 +            WHEN 'Team' THEN 'Neutral'
    172 +            WHEN 'EntityType' THEN 'None'
    173 +            WHEN 'DeathType' THEN 'Normal'
    174 +            WHEN 'VisualScenePath' THEN ''
    175 +            WHEN 'HealthBarHeight' THEN '100'
    176 +            WHEN 'BaseHp' THEN '10'
    177 +            WHEN 'BaseHpRegen' THEN '0'
    178 +            WHEN 'LifeSteal' THEN '0'
    179 +            WHEN 'BaseAttack' THEN '0'
    180 +            WHEN 'BaseAttackSpeed' THEN '100'
    181 +            WHEN 'AttackRange' THEN '0'
    182 +            WHEN 'CritRate' THEN '0'
    183 +            WHEN 'CritDamage' THEN '100'
    184 +            WHEN 'Penetration' THEN '0'
    185 +            WHEN 'BaseDefense' THEN '0'
    186 +            WHEN 'DamageReduction' THEN '0'
    187 +            WHEN 'MoveSpeed' THEN '100'
    188 +            WHEN 'DodgeChance' THEN '0'
    189 +            WHEN 'PickupRange' THEN '300'
    190 +            WHEN 'ExpReward' THEN '1'
    191 +            WHEN 'DetectionRange' THEN '500'
    192 +            WHEN 'IsEnableSpawnRule' THEN 'true'
    193 +            WHEN 'SpawnStrategy' THEN 'Rectangle'
    194 +            WHEN 'SpawnMinWave' THEN '0'
    195 +            WHEN 'SpawnMaxWave' THEN '-1'
    196 +            WHEN 'SpawnInterval' THEN '1'
    197 +            WHEN 'SpawnMaxCountPerWave' THEN '-1'
    198 +            WHEN 'SingleSpawnCount' THEN '1'
    199 +            WHEN 'SingleSpawnVariance' THEN '0'
    200 +            WHEN 'SpawnStartDelay' THEN '0'
    201 +            WHEN 'SpawnWeight' THEN '10'
    202 +            WHEN 'IsShowHealthBar' THEN 'true'
    203 +            WHEN 'IsInvulnerable' THEN 'false'
    204 +            WHEN 'AbilityFeatureGroup' THEN ''
    205 +            WHEN 'FeatureHandlerId' THEN ''
    206 +            WHEN 'Description' THEN ''
    207 +            WHEN 'AbilityIcon' THEN ''
    208 +            WHEN 'AbilityType' THEN 'Passive'
    209 +            WHEN 'AbilityLevel' THEN '1'
    210 +            WHEN 'AbilityMaxLevel' THEN '10'
    211 +            WHEN 'AbilityTriggerMode' THEN 'None'
    212 +            WHEN 'AbilityCostType' THEN 'None'
    213 +            WHEN 'AbilityCostAmount' THEN '0'
    214 +            WHEN 'AbilityCooldown' THEN '0'
    215 +            WHEN 'AbilityDamage' THEN '0'
    216 +            WHEN 'IsAbilityUsesCharges' THEN 'false'
    217 +            WHEN 'AbilityMaxCharges' THEN '0'
    218 +            WHEN 'AbilityChargeTime' THEN '0'
    219 +            WHEN 'AbilityTargetSelection' THEN 'None'
    220 +            WHEN 'AbilityCastRange' THEN '0'
    221 +            WHEN 'AbilityEffectRadius' THEN '0'
    222 +            WHEN 'EffectScene' THEN ''
    223 +            WHEN 'ProjectileScene' THEN ''
    224 +            WHEN 'AbilityChainCount' THEN '3'
    225 +            WHEN 'AbilityChainRange' THEN '300'
    226 +            WHEN 'AbilityChainDelay' THEN '0.2'
    227 +            WHEN 'AbilityChainDamageDecay' THEN '100'
    228 +            WHEN 'SystemId' THEN ''
    229 +            WHEN 'MountGroup' THEN 'Else'
    230 +            WHEN 'Tags' THEN ''
    231 +            WHEN 'Required' THEN 'false'
    232 +            WHEN 'AutoLoad' THEN 'true'
    233 +            WHEN 'StartEnabled' THEN 'true'
    234 +            WHEN 'Priority' THEN '0'
    235 +            WHEN 'AllowedFlowStates' THEN ''
    236 +            WHEN 'RequiredOverlays' THEN ''
    237 +            WHEN 'BlockedOverlays' THEN ''
    238 +            WHEN 'AllowedSimulationStates' THEN ''
    239 +            WHEN 'Dependencies' THEN ''
    240 +            WHEN 'PresetName' THEN 'DefaultPreset'
    241 +            WHEN 'IsActive' THEN 'false'
    242 +            WHEN 'EnabledTags' THEN ''
    243 +            WHEN 'EnabledSystemIds' THEN ''
    244 +            WHEN 'DisabledSystemIds' THEN ''
    245 +            ELSE ''
    246 +        END AS default_value_text,
    247 +        field_key AS display_name
    248 +    FROM (
    249 +        SELECT field_key, value_type
    250 +        FROM field_rows
    251 +        GROUP BY field_key, value_type
    252 +    )
    253 +),
    254 +active_fields AS (
    255 +    SELECT f.*
    256 +    FROM field_rows f
    257 +    JOIN descriptor_source d ON d.field_key = f.field_key
    258 +    LEFT JOIN capability_manifest c ON c.capability_id = d.owner_capability
    259 +    WHERE COALESCE(c.enabled, 1) = 1
    260 +),
    261 +record_docs AS (
    262 +    SELECT
    263 +        r.legacy_table,
    264 +        r.table_id,
    265 +        r.record_id,
    266 +        json_object(
    267 +            'table', r.table_id,
    268 +            'legacyTable', r.legacy_table,
    269 +            'id', r.record_id,
    270 +            'name', COALESCE(NULLIF(MAX(r.display_name), ''), r.record_id),
    271 +            'fields', COALESCE((
    272 +                SELECT json_group_object(f.field_key, json(
    273 +                    CASE
    274 +                        WHEN f.value_type = 'int' THEN json_object('type', f.value_type, 'value', CAST(f.value_text AS INTEGER))
    275 +                        WHEN f.value_type = 'float' THEN json_object('type', f.value_type, 'value', CAST(f.value_text AS REAL))
    276 +                        WHEN f.value_type = 'bool' THEN json_object('type', f.value_type, 'value', json(CASE lower(f.value_text) WHEN 'true' THEN 'true'
          ELSE 'false' END))
    277 +                        ELSE json_object('type', f.value_type, 'value', COALESCE(f.value_text, ''))
    278 +                    END
    279 +                ))
    280 +                FROM active_fields f
    281 +                WHERE f.table_id = r.table_id
    282 +                  AND f.record_id = r.record_id
    283 +                ORDER BY f.field_key
    284 +            ), json('{}')),
    285 +            'legacyData', COALESCE((
    286 +                SELECT json_group_object(
    287 +                    CASE f.field_key
    288 +                        WHEN 'AbilityFeatureGroup' THEN 'FeatureGroupId'
    289 +                        WHEN 'AbilityIcon' THEN 'AbilityIconPath'
    290 +                        WHEN 'EffectScene' THEN 'EffectScenePath'
    291 +                        WHEN 'ProjectileScene' THEN 'ProjectileScenePath'
    292 +                        WHEN 'AbilityChainCount' THEN 'ChainCount'
    293 +                        WHEN 'AbilityChainRange' THEN 'ChainRange'
    294 +                        WHEN 'AbilityChainDelay' THEN 'ChainDelay'
    295 +                        WHEN 'AbilityChainDamageDecay' THEN 'ChainDamageDecay'
    296 +                        ELSE f.field_key
    297 +                    END,
    298 +                    json(
    299 +                        CASE
    300 +                            WHEN f.value_type = 'int' THEN CAST(f.value_text AS INTEGER)
    301 +                            WHEN f.value_type = 'float' THEN CAST(f.value_text AS REAL)
    302 +                            WHEN f.value_type = 'bool' THEN json(CASE lower(f.value_text) WHEN 'true' THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END)
    303 +                            ELSE json_quote(COALESCE(f.value_text, ''))
    304 +                        END
    305 +                    )
    306 +                )
    307 +                FROM active_fields f
    308 +                WHERE f.table_id = r.table_id
    309 +                  AND f.record_id = r.record_id
    310 +                ORDER BY f.field_key
    311 +            ), json('{}'))
    312 +        ) AS doc
    313 +    FROM active_fields r
    314 +    GROUP BY r.legacy_table, r.table_id, r.record_id
    315 +    ORDER BY r.table_id, r.record_id
    316 +),
    317 +descriptor_docs AS (
    318 +    SELECT json_object(
    319 +        'key', d.field_key,
    320 +        'stableKey', d.field_key,
    321 +        'ownerCapability', d.owner_capability,
    322 +        'ownerSkill', lower(d.owner_capability) || '-system',
    323 +        'type', d.descriptor_type,
    324 +        'valueType', d.descriptor_type,
    325 +        'defaultValue', CASE
    326 +            WHEN d.descriptor_type = 'int' THEN CAST(d.default_value_text AS INTEGER)
    327 +            WHEN d.descriptor_type = 'float' THEN CAST(d.default_value_text AS REAL)
    328 +            WHEN d.descriptor_type = 'bool' THEN json(CASE lower(d.default_value_text) WHEN 'true' THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END)
    329 +            ELSE d.default_value_text
    330 +        END,
    331 +        'displayName', d.display_name,
    332 +        'description', '',
    333 +        'iconPath', '',
    334 +        'category', d.owner_capability,
    335 +        'minValue', NULL,
    336 +        'maxValue', NULL,
    337 +        'options', json('[]'),
    338 +        'isPercentage', json('false'),
    339 +        'supportsModifiers', json(CASE
    340 +            WHEN d.field_key IN ('BaseHp', 'BaseHpRegen', 'LifeSteal', 'BaseAttack', 'BaseAttackSpeed', 'AttackRange',
    341 +                'CritRate', 'CritDamage', 'Penetration', 'BaseDefense', 'DamageReduction', 'MoveSpeed', 'DodgeChance',
    342 +                'PickupRange', 'AbilityDamage', 'AbilityDamageBonus', 'CooldownReduction', 'AbilityCooldown',
    343 +                'AbilityChainCount', 'AbilityChainRange', 'AbilityChainDamageDecay') THEN 'true'
    344 +            ELSE 'false'
    345 +        END),
    346 +        'isComputed', json('false')
    347 +    ) AS doc
    348 +    FROM descriptor_source d
    349 +    ORDER BY d.field_key
    350 +),
    351 +resource_docs AS (
    352 +    SELECT json_object(
    353 +        'category', category,
    354 +        'key', resource_key,
    355 +        'path', resource_path,
    356 +        'ownerCapability', owner_capability,
    357 +        'legacyStatus', legacy_status,
    358 +        'sourceTable', source_table,
    359 +        'sourceRowId', source_row_id,
    360 +        'sourceColumn', source_column
    361 +    ) AS doc
    362 +    FROM resource_entry
    363 +    WHERE legacy_status NOT IN ('intentionally-dropped', 'missing')
    364 +    ORDER BY category, resource_key
    365 +),
    366 +counts AS (
    367 +    SELECT
    368 +        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM descriptor_docs) AS descriptor_count,
    369 +        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM record_docs) AS record_count,
    370 +        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM resource_docs) AS resource_count
    371 +)
    372 +SELECT json_object(
    373 +    'schemaVersion', 2,
    374 +    'generatedAtUtc', '$generated_at_utc',
    375 +    'manifest', json_object(
    376 +        'schemaVersion', 2,
    377 +        'generatedAtUtc', '$generated_at_utc',
    378 +        'profile', '$profile',
    379 +        'catalogId', '$catalog_id',
    380 +        'source', 'DataOS/Authoring/slimeainew.authoring.db',
    381 +        'enabledCapabilities', COALESCE((SELECT json_group_array(capability_id) FROM enabled_capabilities), json('[]')),
    382 +        'descriptorCount', (SELECT descriptor_count FROM counts),
    383 +        'recordCount', (SELECT record_count FROM counts),
    384 +        'resourceCount', (SELECT resource_count FROM counts),
    385 +        'validation', json_object('warningCount', 0, 'errorCount', 0)
    386 +    ),
    387 +    'descriptors', COALESCE((SELECT json_group_array(json(doc)) FROM descriptor_docs), json('[]')),
    388 +    'records', COALESCE((SELECT json_group_array(json(doc)) FROM record_docs), json('[]')),
    389 +    'resources', COALESCE((SELECT json_group_array(json(doc)) FROM resource_docs), json('[]'))
    390 +);
    391 +SQL
    392 +
    393 +if command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    394 +    tmp_path="${output_path}.tmp"
    395 +    jq . "$output_path" > "$tmp_path"
    396 +    mv "$tmp_path" "$output_path"
    397 +fi
    398 +
    399 +echo "generated $output_path"

─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• 生成器现在会输出 typed shape。下一步我改 loader：LoadSnapshot 读取 typed document，GetAll<T>() 从 legacyData 或 fields 映射 DTO，ApplyRecordToData 用
  data.Catalog resolve。

• Edited SlimeAINew/Data/RuntimeSnapshot/RuntimeDataSnapshot.cs (+74 -0)
    191      /// <summary>
    192 +    /// 按 DataOS DTO 的 Name 从当前 snapshot 找到 typed record 并应用到 Data。
    193 +    /// <para>返回 false 表示该 config 不是 snapshot-backed DTO，调用方可走迁移 fallback。</para>
    194 +    /// </summary>
    195 +    public static bool TryApplyConfigToData(object config, Data data, out DataApplyReport report)
    196 +    {
    197 +        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(config);
    198 +        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(data);
    199 +
    200 +        report = new DataApplyReport();
    201 +        if (!TryResolveConfigRecord(config, out var table, out var legacyTable, out var recordName))
    202 +        {
    203 +            return false;
    204 +        }
    205 +
    206 +        var snapshot = EnsureSnapshot();
    207 +        var record = snapshot.Records.FirstOrDefault(candidate =>
    208 +            string.Equals(candidate.Table, table, StringComparison.Ordinal)
    209 +            && string.Equals(candidate.Name, recordName, StringComparison.Ordinal)
    210 +            && (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(legacyTable)
    211 +                || string.Equals(candidate.LegacyTable, legacyTable, StringComparison.Ordinal)));
    212 +
    213 +        if (record == null)
    214 +        {
    215 +            report.AddError("snapshot.record_missing", $"Snapshot record not found: table={table}, name={recordName}");
    216 +            return true;
    217 +        }
    218 +
    219 +        report = ApplyRecordToData(snapshot, record.Table, record.Id, data);
    220 +        return true;
    221 +    }
    222 +
    223 +    /// <summary>
    224      /// 清理缓存，供测试或重新生成 snapshot 后刷新。
        ⋮
    316
    317 +    private static bool TryResolveConfigRecord(object config, out string table, out string legacyTable, out string recordName)
    318 +    {
    319 +        table = string.Empty;
    320 +        legacyTable = string.Empty;
    321 +        recordName = string.Empty;
    322 +
    323 +        var configType = config.GetType();
    324 +        if (configType == typeof(PlayerData))
    325 +        {
    326 +            table = "unit.player";
    327 +            legacyTable = "PlayerData";
    328 +        }
    329 +        else if (configType == typeof(EnemyData))
    330 +        {
    331 +            table = "unit.enemy";
    332 +            legacyTable = "EnemyData";
    333 +        }
    334 +        else if (configType == typeof(TargetingIndicatorData))
    335 +        {
    336 +            table = "unit.targeting_indicator";
    337 +            legacyTable = "TargetingIndicatorData";
    338 +        }
    339 +        else if (configType == typeof(ChainAbilityData))
    340 +        {
    341 +            table = "ability";
    342 +            legacyTable = "ChainAbilityData";
    343 +        }
    344 +        else if (configType == typeof(AbilityData))
    345 +        {
    346 +            table = "ability";
    347 +            legacyTable = "AbilityData";
    348 +        }
    349 +        else
    350 +        {
    351 +            return false;
    352 +        }
    353 +
    354 +        var nameProperty = configType.GetProperty(DataKey.Name, BindingFlags.Public | BindingFlags.Instance);
    355 +        recordName = nameProperty?.GetValue(config) as string ?? string.Empty;
    356 +        return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(recordName);
    357 +    }

    289      /// <summary>
    290 +    /// 从 generated runtime snapshot 注册资源条目。
    291 +    /// </summary>
    292 +    /// <param name="entries">待写入的目录条目列表。</param>
    293 +    private static void AddRuntimeSnapshotResourceEntries(List<ResourceCatalogEntry> entries)
    294 +    {
    295 +        foreach (var resource in RuntimeDataSnapshot.GetResources())
    296 +        {
    297 +            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(resource.Key) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(resource.Path))
    298 +            {
    299 +                continue;
    300 +            }
    301 +
    302 +            var category = Enum.TryParse<ResourceCategory>(resource.Category, ignoreCase: false, out var parsedCategory)
    303 +                ? parsedCategory
    304 +                : ResourceCategory.Other;
    305 +            var catalogPath = ResolveRuntimeResourceCatalogPath(resource, category);
    306 +            var entry = new ResourceCatalogEntry(
    307 +                resource.Key, // snapshot resource stable key
    308 +                category, // ResourceManagement 分类
    309 +                resource.Path, // res:// 路径
    310 +                ResolveAssetDisplayName(resource.Path), // UI 显示名
    311 +                catalogPath, // 目录分类路径
    312 +                typeof(PackedScene) // 当前 generated resources 均为场景路径
    313 +            );
    314 +
    315 +            if (!ContainsResourceEntry(entries, entry.ResourceKey, entry.Path))
    316 +            {
    317 +                entries.Add(entry);
    318 +            }
    319 +        }
    320 +    }
    321 +
    322 +    /// <summary>
    323 +    /// 判断目录中是否已有同一个资源条目。
    324 +    /// </summary>
    325 +    /// <param name="entries">已有目录条目。</param>
    326 +    /// <param name="resourceKey">资源稳定键。</param>
    327 +    /// <param name="path">资源路径。</param>
    328 +    private static bool ContainsResourceEntry(
    329 +        IReadOnlyList<ResourceCatalogEntry> entries,
    330 +        string resourceKey,
    331 +        string path)
    332 +    {
    333 +        for (int i = 0; i < entries.Count; i++)
    334 +        {
    335 +            var existing = entries[i];
    336 +            if (string.Equals(existing.ResourceKey, resourceKey, StringComparison.Ordinal)
    337 +                && string.Equals(existing.Path, path, StringComparison.Ordinal))
    338 +            {
    339 +                return true;
    340 +            }
    341 +        }
    342 +
    343 +        return false;
    344 +    }
    345 +
    346 +    /// <summary>
    347 +    /// 为 runtime snapshot resource 推导目录路径。
    348 +    /// </summary>
    349 +    /// <param name="resource">snapshot resource 记录。</param>
    350 +    /// <param name="category">解析后的资源分类。</param>
    351 +    private static string ResolveRuntimeResourceCatalogPath(RuntimeResourceRecord resource, ResourceCategory category)
    352 +    {
    353 +        return category switch
    354 +        {
    355 +            ResourceCategory.AssetEffect => ResolveCatalogPath(resource.Path, EffectRoot, "Effect"),
    356 +            ResourceCategory.AssetUnitEnemy => ResolveCatalogPath(resource.Path, AssetUnitEnemyRoot, "AssetUnit.Enemy"),
    357 +            ResourceCategory.AssetUnitPlayer => ResolveCatalogPath(resource.Path, AssetUnitPlayerRoot, "AssetUnit.Player"),
    358 +            ResourceCategory.AssetProjectile => ResolveCatalogPath(resource.Path, "assets/Projectile", "AssetProjectile"),
    359 +            _ => NormalizeCatalogPath($"RuntimeResource.{category}") ?? UnknownCatalogPath
    360 +        };
    361 +    }
    362 +

    364      /// 尝试从特效资源构建目录条目。

  shim 并统一 resolve 到 catalog key。DataKey 文件会做机械迁移，把 DataMeta 静态字段替换为 DataKey<T>。

  建议顺序
  1. 先读当前状态和 change 上下文：
     - git status --short
     - openspec status --change rewrite-slimeainew-runtime-data-system
     - openspec instructions apply --change rewrite-slimeainew-runtime-data-system --json
  2. 再读上面的必读文档和核心代码。
  3. 根据当前 codebase 事实，判断 typed runtime data 还缺哪一段，不要假设已经完成。
  4. 如果要改代码，优先补 runtime data 主路径，不碰 event 文件。
  5. 最后再跑验证：
     - cd /home/slime/Code/SlimeAI/SlimeAINew
     - dotnet build
     - 需要时再跑 runtime validation scene
     - 回到根目录跑 legacy scan，确认生产 raw string Data.Get/Set 没残留

  已知验证事实
  - 我之前跑过 `dotnet build`，现在因为 event 层回退，出现大量缺失类型错误，典型是：
    - UnitEvents
    - GlobalEvents
    - DataEvents
    - TargetingEvents
    - AbilityEvents
    - UIEvents
  - 所以当前 build 不能当作 runtime data 已完成的证据。
  - 只有 event 层被外部对话补回后，build / scene 才能继续验收。
